[30;1m2454 | [0m[35m`plugins` interface is a very simple plugin manager for installing, listing and uninstalling HTTPie [0m
[30;1m2455 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m2456 | [0m[35mIn the past `pip` was used to install/uninstall plugins, but on some environments (e.g., brew instal[0m
[30;1m2457 | [0m[35mpackages) it wasn’t working properly. The new interface is a very simple overlay on top of `pip` to [0m
[30;1m2458 | [0m[35mplugin installations on every installation method.[0m
[30;1m2459 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m2460 | [0m[35mBy default, the plugins (and their missing dependencies) will be stored under the configuration dire[0m
